# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
- Can be kept anywhere
- Should be cleaned
  every few days ^9hbtI6S2

- Like a personal library
- Rather simple, just information
  about any books, pages or videos ^5Od1tP14

I think there's no relation between 
fleeting and permanent notes. They
shouldn't be connected with line on
this graph. ^jdvl11w9

Don't be limited by the term "permanent".
It's just permanent compared with the 
fleeting ones. ^apsiAD5k

Is basically "studying notes". ^kDnqWPea

讀了半天，感覺卡片盒筆記比較偏向
為「文科研究」設計的。畢竟始祖就
是研究社會學的教授。 ^F3SpJ4rs

- Indexed with n-th lesson
- If you don't know how to take notes,
  maybe it's not even worth doing it. ^SnUZHscG
